        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1266425072" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14967384687533411672"><b>Update November 5th Adding warnings for my friends who expect not only faithful hero but 0% OW activity. Look my warnings at the end of my original review. This is important because this is a book that I recommend all the time to readers who like me hate cheating</b><br/>4.5 solid stars, rounded because this is a great New adult read, FREE OF CHEATING, barely any slutshaming and the hero is just adorable. I've found a new book boyfriend!<br/><br/><br/>Devin Paisley as Garrett!<br/><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472584416i/20211626.png' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Thank you so much my friends of the safety</span>
  <span id="freeText14967384687533411672" style="display:none"><b>Update November 5th Adding warnings for my friends who expect not only faithful hero but 0% OW activity. Look my warnings at the end of my original review. This is important because this is a book that I recommend all the time to readers who like me hate cheating</b><br>4.5 solid stars, rounded because this is a great New adult read, FREE OF CHEATING, barely any slutshaming and the hero is just adorable. I've found a new book boyfriend!<br><br><br>Devin Paisley as Garrett!<br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472584416i/20211626.png" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Thank you so much my friends of the safety gang for giving me information of this book. I was about to pass on this one because the author is the same of that rape fest, disloyal hero fest, antiromantic sex-scenes called Paper princess. I can't believe this is from the same author. Where one book seems to be pro-rape, and is 100% inappropiate for a "YA romance" audience, this book was sexy, romantic, funny, smart (for the most part), realistic from the point of view of an abuse survivor and her strugles, full of anti-rape messages, (almost)free of slutshaming, mature but still addictive in spite of the lack of drama and it was definetely a joy to read. In short the word I'm really looking for to describe this book is AWESOME!<br><br>Garrett is the ideal book-boyfriend if you were looking for one. He manages to be a tortured soul, manwhore without being a cheater or a disgustingly abusive guy! He was so manly and sweet at the same time. And the best is that he had a very funny side. I laughed so much with his wit and his charm. I love him so much that I got pissed of at Hannah for taking a stupid decision later that hurt him so much, but other than that I didn't have problems with this book.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472584784i/20211726.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>All starts when Hannah, an abuse survivor and an "almost-non-TSTL" heroine (TSTL=too stupid to live) agrees to tutor Garrett in exchange of him helping her to get the attention of her crush. I say almost non TSTL because what I noticed from the two Elle Kennedy books I've read is that her heroines are strong for the first part of the book and later they become obedient and go along with the crap others put on them. For 70% of the book I was like "This is going to be a 6 stars" and it wasn't until the end that I had problems with Hannah because <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ she looses her spunk or more like Elle Kennedy makes her lose her spunk. She lets herself be blackmailed and intimated by Garret's father. I wouldn't have even agreed to talk to that horrible man (he beats his wife and beat Garret when he was a kid), but she does it because "otherwise she wouldn't be able to concentrate in work" and then it's obvious that this man wouldn't retire financial support from Garret. I wouldn't have fallen for that, I would have put that man in his place, and even if I had believe his lies, I would have talked to Garret first rather than hurt him. There were so many ways the separation could have gone withouth her turning in a TSTL girl. Not only that. She doesn't talk about this to her friends, and then she lets herself be convinced into talking to a traitorous girl who treated her badly in the past during a recital. I wouldn't have talked to that bitch, but in the same recital Hannah is too agreable to this girl and too cold to her friends <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> but I still would prefer to root for Hannah 100000000 times over Ella, the heroine from the other Kennedy book I read. At least Hannah managed to be FUNNY, AND SMART FOR 80% of the book, she didn't slut-shame and she didn't let Garrett set the tone of the relationship or ordered her around. I love that in heroines.<br><br>Another thing that I love about this book is that sometimes you find adult fiction/erotica marketed as New adult reads, but there's barely any references to college life, to coming of age journeys and to trying to find your place while you're studying. Example of this would be At any price by Breana Audrey. It's labeled NA, but in reality it's more adult/erotica/romantic suspense. I love New adult, I love to see the struggles of people reaching adulthood but not quite there yet. This book is new adult featuring college life, full of college/coming of age situations and in my opinion a must read of the genre.<br><br>The romance builds slowly betweent these two, but it's not completely free of insta-love. I think it has the right rhythm for you to root for these two to be together, it's fast in a way but still you get to know them really well before anything happens. I enjoyed so much that. This book reminds me a lot of Beautiful disaster with the difference that Garrett never considers cheating throughout the customary separation of the couple that happens in all NA reads. Hannah considers cheating, though! But at the end nothing horrible happens and we get our HEA and closure. No cliffhanger here.<br><br>I'm recommending this to romance readers who like me hate TSTLness, cheating heroes, slut shamming and "adult" characters acting like teens. It's been a while since a contemporary romance impressed but The Deal surprised me in a good way, just when I was about to give up on the erotic romance genre.<br><br><b>WARNINGS</b><br>There is OW activity twice. Once the same day H talks h for the first time and another when she's still crushing in another guy but she's slowly falling for hero. I didn't mind. My hard limit is when that happens after our couple kiss for the first time. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ In this book OW happens when they were only strangers and later friends and it wasn't detailed. The first time is fade to black, the second time is a little more visual, I could picture the scene but rather than upsetting me I laughed at it because it was awkward the way Hannah caught him. It didnt' bother me other than I wish Hannah had refused to change their appointment. However, since a lot of my friends hate OW activity and one even didn't finish the book because these scenes I added the warning. I'd say also that I haven't read book 2 but I DNF book 3 because OW activity was too detailed for my taste but that's another free of cheating book, just be careful <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="14967384687533411672" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2209266274" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2209266274" />
    <a title="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale"><img alt="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577855357p2/69106439.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2209266274?book_show_action=true">Dec 09, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥" href="/user/show/69106439-virginia-ronan-herondale">Virginia Ronan ♥ Herondale ♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2209266274" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1535475970990633230"><i>"Sometimes people sneak up on you and suddenly you don’t know how you ever lived without them."</i><br/><br/>A few weeks ago I was in dire need of a funny and sexy read and so I went to my adorable <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/66222749-lia-sunshines-and-penguins' rel='nofollow noopener'>Gansey</a> and asked her for a book recommendation! <br/>This is what she came up with! *lol*<br/><br/>So let me say this before I continue with my review:<br/><br/>Gansey, I’m not disappointed!! XD <br/>You did an amazing job and I’ll definitely consult you in the future! ;-P Thank you!!! =) <br/>And now let’s move on before I get all emotional and act</span>
  <span id="freeText1535475970990633230" style="display:none"><i>"Sometimes people sneak up on you and suddenly you don’t know how you ever lived without them."</i><br /><br />A few weeks ago I was in dire need of a funny and sexy read and so I went to my adorable <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/66222749-lia-sunshines-and-penguins" rel="nofollow noopener">Gansey</a> and asked her for a book recommendation! <br />This is what she came up with! *lol*<br /><br />So let me say this before I continue with my review:<br /><br />Gansey, I’m not disappointed!! XD <br />You did an amazing job and I’ll definitely consult you in the future! ;-P Thank you!!! =) <br />And now let’s move on before I get all emotional and actually start to cry. *lol*<br /><br />This book was everything I wanted it to be and I found myself laughing out loud so much it was almost creepy! Well, okay I suppose it actually <u>
  <b>was</b>
</u> creepy for the people who saw me reading it. *lol* But I just couldn’t help myself! <br />Hannah and Garret were just too much fun to read about and even though “The Deal” deals (no pun intended, I swear ;-P) with some serious topics as well, it was still a fluffy and nice read! XD This is definitely one of those books that make you giggle like a lunatic and cause you to roll your eyes like an angry bull! <br /><br /><i>“The second I encounter his erection, my jaw drops.<br />“Oh my God, are you kidding me?”<br />He looks startled. “What’s wrong?”<br />“Are you taking human growth hormones or something? I snatch my hand back, fighting another rush of nervousness. “There’s no way that huge man monster is fitting inside me!”<br />Garrett’s head abruptly drops in the crook of his arm as a shudder racks his body. At first I think he’s pissed off. Or maybe even crying. It takes several seconds before I realize what’s happening. He’s laughing. Scratch that – he’s in hysterics.”</i><br /><br />Yes, there were a lot of clichés in this story but truth be told, that was its appeal! &lt;3 Well, at least for me it was! ;-) Sometimes you just need a nice book to escape your own world and “The Deal” definitely delivered! XD<br />I could go on and on about how cocky and self-confident Garret was or how amazing and strong Hannah acted, but I think I’ll just leave it at that! ;-)<br /><br />If you’re looking for a nice and witty romance that will make you laugh and give you some sexy shivers, this is exactly the right book for you! If you’re tired of clichés and prefer your boys without a taut and sexy six-pack (Who does?!) you better don’t read it though. *lol* <br /><br /><b>“The Deal”</b> is book one of the “Off-Campus” series and I’m definitely going to read the other books as well. Because let’s face the truth: Some of Garret’s hot roomies have already captured my interest (Tucker!! You hot boy you!!) and I really can’t wait to read their individual stories! XD<br /><br />Happy Reading!!! =)<br /><br /><i>“It’s like that pond I skated on when I was a kid—from a distance, the ice looked so shiny and smooth, until you got close enough to it, and suddenly all the uneven edges and crisscrossed skate marks became visible. That’s me, I guess. Covered with skate marks that nobody ever seems to notice.”</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="1535475970990633230" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1226500718" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1226500718" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1226500718?book_show_action=true">Mar 13, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs">Amy | Foxy Blogs</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1226500718" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13104406673436524388"><b>*Just about 4 Stars* — Great read! </b><br/><br/><i>
  <b>The Deal</b>
</i> is the perfect choice when you’re looking for something engaging, sexy, and light—with a lil' dose of depth to trigger your emotions.<br/><br/>YES, those who claim this book contains cliches aren’t kidding. There are certainly plenty of cliched one-liners to go around, but for some reason, I was able to glide right past them.<br/><br/>And… <i>
  <b>okay</b>
</i>…so maybe just about <i>everyone</i> in this book is totally hot, and the storyline was often predictable…<br/><br/><b>Am I selling you on thi</b></span>
  <span id="freeText13104406673436524388" style="display:none"><b>*Just about 4 Stars* — Great read! </b><br><br><i>
  <b>The Deal</b>
</i> is the perfect choice when you’re looking for something engaging, sexy, and light—with a lil' dose of depth to trigger your emotions.<br><br>YES, those who claim this book contains cliches aren’t kidding. There are certainly plenty of cliched one-liners to go around, but for some reason, I was able to glide right past them.<br><br>And… <i>
  <b>okay</b>
</i>…so maybe just about <i>everyone</i> in this book is totally hot, and the storyline was often predictable…<br><br><b>Am I selling you on this book yet? </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422912232ra/13562967.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>
  <b>But, here’s where I think this story truly thrived</b>
</u>:<br><br><b>It was so much freaking fun!</b> <br><br>I laughed…<br>I swooned…<br>I wanted to be friends with the majority of the characters and <b>drop-kick</b> the rest! <br>I'd put the book down and couldn't wait to pick it back up again.<br><br>This story hooked me with<i>out</i> the presence of a highly original plot, and I think there’s something major to be said about that. <br><br>It's simple, and doesn't try too hard or bombard us with a dozen over-the-top scenarios—and I really enjoyed that. <br><br>The characters are incredibly entertaining and allow you to warm up to them immediately. Their flaws are intense without feeling forced, and quickly become endearing. <br><br>This is one of those books that invites you to just sit back and enjoy the ride. And even though it’s not completely smooth sailing, the tension-filled angst wasn't overdone, and added much excitement.<br><br><b>A pinch of the plot, since the blurb in this case does its job well:</b> Music major, Hannah, has been through a traumatic event—one that has basically crippled her love life, and for good reason. <br><br>But she forges ahead and soon her sights are set on the school’s star football player, <b>Justin</b>. Only, there’s no way Justin would ever notice someone with her lowly social status...<br><br>So when the very “popular”, very sexy, and very flirty lady’s man, <b>Garret</b>, offers to help Hannah gain the attention of her crush in exchange for some Ethics tutoring, “The Deal” is born…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380905634ra/3153558.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The sexy trail of events that take place after are nothing short of <b>awesome</b>, and the perspectives alternating between hero and heroine are implemented with distinguishability, as well as believability. <br><br><b>Slight gripe:</b>As much as I enjoyed this read, there was a certain “trigger” incorporated that I became a bit conflicted with. <i>Click spoiler to see trigger: </i><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ we find out early on that heroine was raped in past <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>On the one hand, this element was vital in explaining certain behavior, but there were times it seemed to lack a little conviction. <br><br>HOWEVER, that’s just <i>this</i> gal’s opinion, as I’m certain others will perceive this aspect quite differently. <br><br>In sum, I would 100% recommend this book to anyone who longs for a little fun in their romantic fiction. And for all you book-boyfriend collectors—this hero <b>DOES NOT</b> disappoint!<br><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪  Genre/Category:</b> Romance/New Adult<br><b>▪  Steam Caliber:</b> Quite steamy<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Slow build. Enemies, to friends, to lovers.<br><b>▪  Characters:</b> Well fleshed out and lovable.<br><b>▪  Plot:</b> Hero makes a deal with heroine to help gain the attention of her crush. College setting. <br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Simplistic and fun. Humorous.<br><b>▪ POV:</b> 1st Person: Alternating perspectives between hero and heroine.<br><b>▪  Cliffhanger:</b> Nope! Complete story.<br><b>▪  Next Installment:</b> Spinoff (Logan)<br><b>▪  HEA? </b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yep! ;) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412050368i/11316768.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Pretty-Words-Book-Blog/860331017317983" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height='“40"' width="150" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413062455i/11461733._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1768379932" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13256663066925560085"><b>First Read:</b> 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br/><b>Second Read:</b> 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br/><b>Third Read:</b> 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟 <br/><br/>THIRD TIME’S A CHARM 😂 can someone tell me where I can find a guy like garrett from? <br/><br/>Ahhhhh, I LOVE 💙 this series❗️Complete trash for Garrett 😍<br/><br/>••••••••••••••••••<br/><br/>( Original Review ) <br/><br/><i>First read of 2017! *whoop whoop*</i><br/><br/><b>Rating:</b> ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ / 5 stars<br/><b>Lead Male Character:</b> ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ / 5 stars<br/><b>Lead Female Character:</b> ★ ★ ★ ★ / 5 stars<br/><b>Plotline:</b> ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ / 5 stars<br/><b>Genre:</b> Sports (hockey) and romance <br/><b>Will I recommend this book to others?:</b> Hell yeah! <br/><b>Will I rerea</b></span>
  <span id="freeText13256663066925560085" style="display:none"><b>First Read:</b> 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br><b>Second Read:</b> 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟<br><b>Third Read:</b> 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟 <br><br>THIRD TIME’S A CHARM 😂 can someone tell me where I can find a guy like garrett from? <br><br>Ahhhhh, I LOVE 💙 this series❗️Complete trash for Garrett 😍<br><br>••••••••••••••••••<br><br>( Original Review ) <br><br><i>First read of 2017! *whoop whoop*</i><br><br><b>Rating:</b> ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ / 5 stars<br><b>Lead Male Character:</b> ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ / 5 stars<br><b>Lead Female Character:</b> ★ ★ ★ ★ / 5 stars<br><b>Plotline:</b> ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ / 5 stars<br><b>Genre:</b> Sports (hockey) and romance <br><b>Will I recommend this book to others?:</b> Hell yeah! <br><b>Will I reread this book?:</b> Absolutely! <br><b>Overall story summed up in one word:</b> Garrett-tastic! ;)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444159586ra/16460711.gif" width="500" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"'Are you taking human growth hormones or something? There's no way that huge man monster is fitting inside me!'"</i>
</b><br><br>This book was definitely what I needed at the moment. Since Christmas, I was in a reading slump and I wanted something fun and light, maybe a romance novel to get me back into the mood of reading. Looking through my TBR list, I came upon this one and decided that this would be perfect! There were many glowing reviews and of course, I had to see what everyone was talking about. And can I just say, <b>I wasn't in the least bit disappointed with this one.</b> In fact, I'm not in a slump anymore so this worked perfectly! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1483335712ra/21602078.gif" width="500" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"'I'm hot for you, Garrett. Only you.'"</i>
</b><br><br><b>My first <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1935000.Elle_Kennedy" title="Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">Elle Kennedy</a> book and <u>definitely</u> not my last!</b> When I first started <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24920901.The_Deal__Off_Campus___1_" title="The Deal (Off-Campus, #1) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">The Deal</a>, I'll admit, it sounded pretty cliche-y, you know? Where the shy and nobody girl has this big crush on the football jock and enlists the help of a friend or some other jock to help get his attention, they fall in love, and BAM! End of story. But, it was just so funny and I <i>had</i> to keep going. Hannah and Garrett has this chemistry about them that just makes me smile like an idiot. <i>If only I knew a guy like Garrett, it'd be heaven...</i> Anyways, this book didn't make me smile or chuckle, but it downright made me howl in laughter. I always love a good romance novel with humor in it :D <br><br>Not to mention, those sex scenes were oh so steamy! Garrett is just <b>ahhhhhhh-mazing</b>, especially in bed. <i>*waggles eyebrows*</i> <br><br>Plus, I read the majority of this on January 1st, the same day as Garrett's birthday :D <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1476733446ra/20875025.gif" width="500" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"'I love you, Garrett.'"</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1483335712i/21602079.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"'I love you, Hannah.'"</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1483335712i/21602080.jpg" width="500" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"I don't look back these days. I only look forward."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1483335712i/21602081.jpg" width="500" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Everything about this book was perfect, from the different characters, to the plot, and the conflict, I enjoyed every minute of it! Garrett is sexy and Hannah is one lucky girl to have a guy like him!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13256663066925560085" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer9950790487528580522">the whole <i>fake dating to real dating</i> isnt my favourite trope. usually because it deals with childish games, playing 'hard to get,' and making people jealous. im not a fan of those kind of dating tactics (maybe thats why im single) but this pleasantly surprised me.<br/><br/>the highlight of this story is definitely the interactions and chemistry between hannah and garrett. their banter is relatable and i actually believed the feelings between them. it was so adorable to see how they grew into liking each o</span>
  <span id="freeText9950790487528580522" style="display:none">the whole <i>fake dating to real dating</i> isnt my favourite trope. usually because it deals with childish games, playing 'hard to get,' and making people jealous. im not a fan of those kind of dating tactics (maybe thats why im single) but this pleasantly surprised me.<br /><br />the highlight of this story is definitely the interactions and chemistry between hannah and garrett. their banter is relatable and i actually believed the feelings between them. it was so adorable to see how they grew into liking each other. i mean, the blurb doesnt do this story justice. i enjoyed how this went deeper than just fake dating - its actually a pretty solid story. maybe not the best writing out there, but quite entertaining. <br /><br />im looking forward to eventually continuing the series because i guess hockey bros are now my thing? lol.<br /><br /><b>↠ <i>3.5 stars</i></b></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1509588666" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5315211199007901334"> <blockquote>
<i><b>"One day I was telling him to get lost, the next, I'm snuggling in bed with him. Life is so frickin' weird sometimes."</b></i> </blockquote><br/><br/><b>WOW! WHY DIDN'T I PICK THIS BOOK UP EARLIER?</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1453006968ra/17771347.gif' width='350' height='230' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24920901.The_Deal__Off_Campus___1_' title='The Deal (Off-Campus, #1) by Elle Kennedy' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Deal</a> proves to be a huge surprise in the best sense possible. It's such a great New Adult book complete with all the elements that can make you swoon like crazy! I had so much fun reading this book. I have been eye-ing this for about a year now and I have to say that I did regret why it took me so long to dive into it.<br/><br/>I was imme</span>
  <span id="freeText5315211199007901334" style="display:none"> <blockquote>
<i><b>"One day I was telling him to get lost, the next, I'm snuggling in bed with him. Life is so frickin' weird sometimes."</b></i> </blockquote><br><br><b>WOW! WHY DIDN'T I PICK THIS BOOK UP EARLIER?</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1453006968ra/17771347.gif" width="350" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24920901.The_Deal__Off_Campus___1_" title="The Deal (Off-Campus, #1) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">The Deal</a> proves to be a huge surprise in the best sense possible. It's such a great New Adult book complete with all the elements that can make you swoon like crazy! I had so much fun reading this book. I have been eye-ing this for about a year now and I have to say that I did regret why it took me so long to dive into it.<br><br>I was immediately wrapped up in this story the moment I started it, because why not? Apart from the balls to the walls <b>humor</b> that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1935000.Elle_Kennedy" title="Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">Elle Kennedy</a> put into this book, the characters made it even more interesting. The heroine <b>Hannah Wells</b> and the lover boy, Ice Hockey team captain of Briar University <b>Garrett Graham</b> are both fun and enjoyable to read. The oozing chemistry, the good-natured bickering, and the sexual tension-- why, they're both PERFECT! I can't even find any flaw with them because Hannah is one strong-willed character (despite of what happened to her in the past) while Garrett is typically the man of your dreams! I find his cockiness and sarcasm combined with his sweetness and charm a total turn-on. And my, the way he treats Hannah and calls her <i>"Wellsy"</i>... I can't even!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398973810ra/9491469.gif" width="360" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What I especially loved about this book was the <b>relationship development</b> between Hannah and Garrett. Some books fail to convince me on how the characters fell in love with each other because of the very insta-love thingy that goes on, but in this book, there was perfect timing: from complete strangers- to friends - to close friends - to f*ck buddies (lol) - to boyfriends-girlfriends. Both of them didn't instantly feel that 'connection' and 'spark' but in the long run, SURPRISE! The romance was unhurried and was developed naturally and it just made me feel thrilled on how they're going to fall in love.<br><br> <blockquote>
<i><b>Sometimes people sneak up on you and suddenly you don't know how you ever lived without them.</b></i> </blockquote><br><br>And even though the book conveys heavy subject matters such as abuse, the author made everything sound lighter here because of the hilarious dialogues and the quirky, entertaining side-characters such as <b>Logan</b>, <b>Dean</b>, <b>Tucker</b>, <b>Allie</b>, etc.<br><br>This book, as a whole, is absolutely 5-star worthy! It made me laugh and swoon the entire time which made it so hard for me to put it down. I believe I have just found a new favorite book and it's because of the unbelievably humorous and delicious writing style of Elle Kennedy. <br><br>Note to self: Read more books written by her.<br><br>Rating:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445993136i/16730745.jpg" width="200" height="45" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><p>
  <a href="https://bibliopearl.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446199662i/16763926._SX540_.jpg" alt="Pearl's Book Journey (1)" width="380" height="190" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</p><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445993261i/16730770.jpg" width="200" height="120" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

<div id="review_1201019883" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1201019883" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1201019883?book_show_action=true">Feb 14, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Elle Kennedy Fans, Hockey, NA, Romance</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1201019883" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18094126951161702323"><b>5 Face Palming, HardCore Loving Stars<br/> * * * * * <i>Spoiler Free</i> OMG OMG OMG THIS IS FREE!!!!<br/>Elle Kennedy has been a go-to author for me whenever I wanted something with an easy to follow plot and a very sensual, spicy, sexy man. The woman would be complete, not weak, focused, either on work, relationship... or lack thereof... and have friends to back her up. Real people... with love stories that were HOT! In all of her work I have read...I felt she had a very keen grasp on what worked for these sto</b></span>
  <span id="freeText18094126951161702323" style="display:none"><b>5 Face Palming, HardCore Loving Stars<br> * * * * * <i>Spoiler Free</i> OMG OMG OMG THIS IS FREE!!!!<br>Elle Kennedy has been a go-to author for me whenever I wanted something with an easy to follow plot and a very sensual, spicy, sexy man. The woman would be complete, not weak, focused, either on work, relationship... or lack thereof... and have friends to back her up. Real people... with love stories that were HOT! In all of her work I have read...I felt she had a very keen grasp on what worked for these stories. In other words, if I was reading a Kennedy... I knew I was in good hands. <br><br>Well, Ms. Kennedy has written one of the best New Adult "college" stories I have read. She has taken all of the normal conflicts...and then raised the bar. Because her characters are two complete, fully formed adults. They have purpose; they have attainable goals. They have experienced individually horrible situations and through their inner strength worked to be as Whole as they can. They do not whine; they do not play "the woe is me card"... and they would have every single reason to. No... they confronted their demons, worked to "get over" them and are ready to get on with life.<br><br>Let's pause for a moment and give thanks... ok.</b><br><br>We have Hannah; from a small town with two loving, everyday parents. They both work and support the career goals of their talented singer/songwriter daughter. They were middle class, worked hard to own a home and be part of a community. Due to a horrific event with Hannah... they lost everything... they lost their financial security, their standing in the community and church and their freedom to leave due to the housing crisis. They cannot sell, so both parents are working low end jobs and getting by. <br><br>With all of that, though, they stand behind their daughter... give her the emotional support she needs and just are there for her even though they are miles away. It is with this type of love, Hannah is who she is. She is a girl who has been challenged like many... hurt like many, yet through counseling and fortitude, learned to do as she was guided... "Take Baby Steps". She is a very pretty, natural girl. Extremely talented in the musical arts and when she sings the world drops away. She is a junior in the music program at Briar University on full scholarship. This does not pay for her food, books and other living expenses. She also waits tables at a 50's inspired diner not far from campus. She shares her dorm room with her friend who is always trying to get her out and to parties. They both look after each other. <br><br>Hannah has had some experience with guys but nothing has given her the feelings she is able to get on her own...it is like she is blocked... or in her words... broken. The only interest she has had lately in the opposite sex is this new Football player on Campus... he fights the usually image by letting it be known he loves Hemingway! Hannah has a class with him... stares at him from behind pages and gets tongue tied whenever an opportunity should happen for her to talk with him. <br><br>She is in this daze when Garrett Graham knocks into her...UGH...he is the Big man on Campus... Captain of the Hockey team and gorgeous... pantie- dropping-I-want gorgeous. Every woman on campus wants him; whether as a Puck Bunny... because of the status of doing a player... or because he is beautiful man meat...and the status of doing him and what he will be in the future... Because he is on the fast track to Pro Hockey... at least he was until this friggin class with this sub teacher... A class which was supposed to be easy but now is going to ruin his GPA and keep him off the team. <br><br>Garrett comes from Hockey royalty... his father is famous..a record breaking professional player with an image the public loves... too bad the public doesn't know about the private person; the controlling, abusive man who drilled Garrett day in and day out since he could hold a stick. For Garrett, he hates the man for what he has done to his mother, to him and to the game...but the one saving grace is the ice and game... for his real family is his team. He is a senior and soon he will be on his way... able to fly on the ice, able to breathe finally away from the control of his dad... so he cannot let any F mess with the goals so close within reach.<br><br>With an F to make up and the scattered mess he made of Hannah's stuff... he sees an A on her midterm paper. Garrett knows what must happen... he needs Hannah to tutor him for the make up exam... and he is determined to have her do it. When he makes up his mind about anything... there is no end until he reaches his goal... <br><br>Hannah has no use for Garrett. She has no desire to be around him or help him. She has experienced with her arts/drama click how the "Jocks" treat them... no thank you. She has other things on her mind... like pursuing her football guy.<br><br>She shuts down Garrett as nicely as she can... and he is stunned... he uses the puppy dog eyed look..nothing. He uses the sweet smile... not a budge... he will have to re group. He goes to her diner and sits in her area. Damn... she has to wait on him... again... nothing he says is working... she won't take money, says she has no time because of her winter program contest with a $5,000 win...he is getting flustered...and then it hits him....<br><br>Mr. Football... He knows she is interested in this guy...and knows he has the bait... he will pretended date her so she is seen as taken, popular and out of reach... everything a guys sees and makes him interested. It takes some convincing but finally Hannah is on board. She will only tutor him for this one make up mid term...he will take her around to a frat party he knows this guy will be ... make it look like they are together and hook her up with a date with her goal guy. Easy peasey....<br><br>Except we all know what is coming... don't we...<br><br>Well, what happens next may follow the outline of these types of college stories... But really doesn't because what happens next is written with such humor, crass, fun and then most importantly Grace... yes grace...<br><br>Because both these two have scar tissue to work through... hidden secrets which are revealed each other... and in this getting to know one another...a true and authentic friendship develops over time. Joking and hanging out. Becoming friends with Garrett's team members. Garrett appreciating all the beauty and talent which is Hannah... no affectations... no hidden agendas, just an amazing woman who is honest and caring. Who see him not as just the hockey star but as the guy who is smart, loves history and applies himself. <br><br>There are secondary issues addressed in this story besides the love story of these two... and they intertwine seamlessly. They address all of the ugly in the world; parental violence, domestic abuse, sexual violence, bullying and drugging. All of these factors could have been over done or felt like an add on... but as I said earlier... this story had the deft hand of Kennedy and we were lead through all of this well. <br><br>I would be remiss if I did not mention how sensual, hot and down right bookorgasmic the scenes were between Garrett and Hannah. This was not inst-lust... this was a slow build to real. Garrett was a dream man... and the care and instincts he used in handling what was presented to him by Hannah was perfect...and hot and steamy... and laundry inducing.<br><br>So what we have here is a New Adult book which treats its readers as if they are smart enough to follow a story without being manipulated unnecessarily. Is there some angst... yes. Is there some conflict... yes. BUT is it resolved without gut wrenching long drawn out mindless crazy. It happens and then it is fixed.<br><br>The fantastic news is this is the first in a new series for Kennedy. All of the secondary characters here were interesting and have enough personalities to give us stories to come. I cannot wait.<br><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24920901.The_Deal__Off_Campus___1_" title="The Deal (Off-Campus, #1) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1431282052s/24920901.jpg" alt="The Deal (Off-Campus, #1) by Elle Kennedy" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>The Deal (Off-Campus, #1)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1201019883">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25564665.The_Mistake__Off_Campus___2_" title="The Mistake (Off-Campus, #2) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1447598937s/25564665.jpg" alt="The Mistake (Off-Campus, #2) by Elle Kennedy" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> The Mistake (Off-Campus, #2)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1213223269">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27252717.The_Score__Off_Campus___3_" title="The Score (Off-Campus, #3) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1493326480s/27252717.jpg" alt="The Score (Off-Campus, #3) by Elle Kennedy" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> The Score (Off-Campus, #3)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1267792142">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28262024.The_Goal__Off_Campus___4_" title="The Goal (Off-Campus, #4) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1477069102s/28262024.jpg" alt="The Goal (Off-Campus, #4) by Elle Kennedy" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> The Goal (Off-Campus, #4)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1506928328">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a></b><br><br><b>~~~~~ Before Reading ~~~~~</b><br><b>
  <i>Do most NA books make you want to bang your head against a wall?<br><br>Do you get annoyed with male and female characters who should just know better and get a clue?<br><br>Well, I am here to announce Elle Kennedy has broken the barriers of the NA curse... She has written a smart, compelling and real book about college seniors who you fall for hook, line and sinker at first meeting....<br><br>Oh... did I mention our guy is the captain of the Hockey team...and the gal... the best little singer/musician with wit, charm and strength.<br><br>And meet them you will... closer to review time...</i>
</b><br><br><i>A gifted copy was provided by author/publisher for an honest review.</i><br> <br><strong>For more Reviews, Free E-books and Giveaways</strong><br><div>

<span id="freeTextContainer8257310305905881469"><strong>Sweet, Heart-Warming College Love Story</strong><br/><br/>This was a fairly light-hearted and humorous love story with a HEA. Although it was extremely predictable, it was entertaining and heartfelt. Sometimes, predictable is alright and that was the case for this book.<br/><br/>Garrett is a star hockey player at school. He aggressively pursues Hannah, a more reserved music major, after seeing that she aced a test in a shared class. His poor score on the test will drop his GPA and result in him being benched, if he can't ac</span>
  <span id="freeText8257310305905881469" style="display:none"><strong>Sweet, Heart-Warming College Love Story</strong><br /><br />This was a fairly light-hearted and humorous love story with a HEA. Although it was extremely predictable, it was entertaining and heartfelt. Sometimes, predictable is alright and that was the case for this book.<br /><br />Garrett is a star hockey player at school. He aggressively pursues Hannah, a more reserved music major, after seeing that she aced a test in a shared class. His poor score on the test will drop his GPA and result in him being benched, if he can't ace the make-up exam. Hannah isn't interested in tutoring the arrogant jock. He's not interested in anyone else and won't take no for an answer. Eventually, the two strike a deal and the rest is history. <br /><br />I can't say that I fell in love with this book, but I liked it. It took me a little while to actually like the characters, but once I did, they kept me constantly entertained. Garrett, in particular, kept me laughing with his chauvinistic false bravado. If you're looking for a light-hearted, college-aged romance, this might be a good choice for you.<br /><br />Check out more of my reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.bookaddicthaven.com">www.bookaddicthaven.com</a> </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1212456107" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4901599514694927734">￼<br/><br/>|4.5 stars|<br/><br/>Well, she got the orgasm. She did. And I know I’m going to get the sex. I will. But right now, all I want is for this girl to smile at me again.<br/>￼<br/><br/>I fell in love with Garrett. Big time.<br/><br/>I had so much fun reading this book I'm still smiling like an idiot and my cheeks hurt.<br/><br/>Alright so The Deal tells Hannah Wells' story and how she's going to get her crush's attention. She's in college and she's major in Vocal Performance, she's got a hard past but she won't let anything ruin her oportunit</span>
  <span id="freeText4901599514694927734" style="display:none">￼<br /><br />|4.5 stars|<br /><br />Well, she got the orgasm. She did. And I know I’m going to get the sex. I will. But right now, all I want is for this girl to smile at me again.<br />￼<br /><br />I fell in love with Garrett. Big time.<br /><br />I had so much fun reading this book I'm still smiling like an idiot and my cheeks hurt.<br /><br />Alright so The Deal tells Hannah Wells' story and how she's going to get her crush's attention. She's in college and she's major in Vocal Performance, she's got a hard past but she won't let anything ruin her oportunity to finally talk to Justin Kohl. Things, however, aren't easy and on top of that Hockey star Garrett Graham keeps following her around in hopes he can get her to tutor him in a class. He needs better grades, she needs Justin's attention and when a deal is on the table Hannah has to decide if she's going to do anything to achieve her ultimate goal but when feelings are involved nothing is black and white.<br /><br />￼<br /><br />You have no idea how much I enjoyed this book. Oh my gods, I laughed so hard I almost pissed myself and I also was very frustrated and I was mad, sad, in love... I mean, The Deal became, in one night, in one of my favorites stories. I'm so happy I read this book.<br /><br />First we have Hannah, who's lusting over Justin and yeah, that was kinda silly but crushes ofter are. She's an amazing singer and she's quite smart and gosh she's sarcastic. I loved her. She's dealing with her life after she was raped years ago but she's over that. Like, those kind of things are absolutely hard to get over but she's determined and she won't let what happened ruin her life. She's moved on but yeah, she's wary and you can't blame her for that. Thing is she doesn't have a happy sex life and men don't turn her on that easily but just the sight of Justin gets her all ready. I can relate to insta-lust so yeah, I saw where she was coming from and this Justin guy is pretty hot but she thinks the man walks on water for fuck's sake. That was one of the three things that bothered me about her. She doesn't even talk to the guy but whoa he's like the ultimate hot boy to her. Ugh...<br />￼<br />The other two things are that she can be really blind and she doesn not comunicate that well.<br /><br />But She's pretty cool and have some pretty cool friends and in some ways she was very relateable so I truly had no major issues with her. I liked that she was bold and shy at the same time but she was also cute and sexy and caring. I really really liked the girl.<br /><br />Then we got Garrett.<br />*sigh*<br /><br />Garrett's such a jackass. He's not mean but he's kinda assholerish. I like that in people, what can I say? He was cocky as hell and stubborn but he's got a big heart. <br />I knew he was hiding something so, when it finally came out, I was happy. Not happy that it happened to him but happy that I could, somehow, undertood the guy. He loves playing hockey but what he really wants is to stop living under his father shadow. <br />That man was a sick bastard and deserve to go to hell.<br />I wasn't thrilled about the whole "I'm a man" concept, though. I saw it several times in the book and I don't think that being "a man" can be used as an excuse to have sex or do things. If you're attracted to that person that's it. And I think that's the only thing I didn't like about him because I was oh so drooling over the rest of him.<br />He was sexy and confident and he didn't run away from his feelings and he knew what he wanted. <br />￼<br /><br />And the sex scenes? They were actually cute and hot and really funny. I loved their dynamic. I loved that they trust in each other that much.<br />￼<br /><br />When I learned what happened to Hannah I was a bit afraid I wasn't going to be that into the book just because I happen to love Wait For You by J. Lynn and both book were similar but nope. This one was sexier and darker and I loved it. Something weird happened, though. Even when I finished the book in one setting and I flew through the pages I felt the book was longer than it actually was. +38 chapter? Damn...<br /><br />Anyway, this is book one so I think that book two is going to be about Logan. Right? Because I don't think Kennedy can add more stuff on this couple without screwing things up. Don't get me wrong, I want to read more about them but a second book will only add drama and I'm happy with how things are now. So yeah, I think it'll be Logan and I don't know if the rest of the books are going to continue with Dean and Tucker but why not.<br />￼<br /><br />|UPDATE 06/05/2015|<br /><br />It was Logan, lol.<br /><br />The best thing that I could do after reading The Mistake was re-reading this book. I appreciate how strong Hannah is now, like I appreciate it even more and how absolutely adorable Garrett is and how solid is his friendship with Logan and Dean and Tucker.<br /><br />There is no doubt I will be re-reading the whole series, once all the books are out, over and over because they're just that good.</span>

<div id="review_1211546949" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1211546949" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1211546949?book_show_action=true">Feb 25, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=sports-romance">sports-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=new-adult-mania">new-adult-mania</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=college-romance">college-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1211546949" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2361429610966129421">11/22/16 edit<br/>I've been rereading romance favorites and I forgot how much I loved this one!!! Makes me want to reread the whole series!<br/>******************************************<br/>February 2015:<br/><b> 4.5-5 Wellsy stars! </b><br/><br/><b> <i> "The ice looked so shiny and smooth, until you got close enough to it, and suddenly all the uneven edges and crisscrossed skate marks became visible. That’s me, I guess. Covered with skate marks that nobody ever seems to notice.” </i> </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/the%20deal.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425177462i/13857580.png' alt=' photo the deal.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This is one of those books that really does live up </span>
  <span id="freeText2361429610966129421" style="display:none">11/22/16 edit<br>I've been rereading romance favorites and I forgot how much I loved this one!!! Makes me want to reread the whole series!<br>******************************************<br>February 2015:<br><b> 4.5-5 Wellsy stars! </b><br><br><b> <i> "The ice looked so shiny and smooth, until you got close enough to it, and suddenly all the uneven edges and crisscrossed skate marks became visible. That’s me, I guess. Covered with skate marks that nobody ever seems to notice.” </i> </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/the%20deal.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425177462i/13857580.png" alt=" photo the deal.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is one of those books that really does live up to the hype! We've all been seeing this book passed around, and normally I'm skeptical when it's a book everyone loves because most of the time I end up hating it, but not in this case.<br><br><b> The Deal </b> starts out like your typical new adult romance but it's so much more. There's a girl at college who has issues, which are said straight away at the beginning (something I actually liked knowing up front so it wasn't dragged out as a plot point) and a jock who needs tutoring help. Hannah is a music major and one of the few people acing her ethics test. She has a gigantic crush on a football player who doesn't know she exists. Garrett is the school star hockey player and just failed his midterm, so he needs Hannah's help.<br><br>So many people have done wonderful reviews and there's no way I could live up to them, so I'm breaking this down into what I loved about the book, because there really isn't anything I didn't like about it.<br><br>-The banter. There were so many great one liners disbursed throughout this gem. I was reading them out loud to any of my friends who were in my vicinity. Here's one example:<br><br><b> <i> “Just out of curiosity,” she says, “after you wake up in the morning, do you admire yourself in the mirror for one hour or two?” <br>“Two,” I reply cheerfully. <br>“Do you high five yourself?” <br>“Of course not.” I smirk. “I kiss each of my biceps and then point to the ceiling and thank the big man upstairs for creating such a perfect male specimen.” </i> </b><br><br>-The writing in general. This book flowed beautifully and I read 66% of it in practically a few hours! Had to force myself to go to bed before continuing on. The author had a sense of humor I just connected with.<br><br><b> <i> “If this was a movie, she’d be the young, ambitious teacher who shows up at the inner city school and inspires the fuckups, and suddenly everyone’s putting down their AKs and picking up their pencils, and the end credits scroll up to announce how all the kids got into Harvard or some shit. Instant Oscar for Hilary Swank.” </i> </b><br><br>-The characters. Many have said that Hannah was annoying at first, but I think I have a pretty high tolerance for annoying females because she didn't bother me at all. Sure she wasn't into Garrett when she first met him, but this book and this story wouldn't be what it is if she had. Garrett liked that she wasn't a puck slut, and he had to fight to get her to even talk to him. The character development between the two of them was extremely well done.<br><br>And Garrett, oh Garrett.<br><a href="http://reactiongifs.com/?p=8007" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425177462ra/13857581.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Love him! He's earned a spot among my book boyfriends!!!<br><br>**I would have liked more steam and a bit more angst, but I'm a gigantic angst whore and can eat up giant doses and demand more. So for everyone else this is probably the perfect amount of angst.<br><br>Thanks <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1211670189?book_show_action=false&amp;ref=ru_lihp_up_rv_0_mclk-up2211635201" rel="nofollow noopener"> Jasmine </a> for the buddy read! I think we both devoured this too quickly to go super in depth but it was lots of fun :)<br><br>My parting words to you all:<br><br><b> <i> “Penises!<br>Sweet Jesus.<br>Penises everywhere.<br>Horror slams into me as I register what I'm seeing. Oh God. I've stumbled onto a penis convention. Big penises and small penises and fat penises and penis-shaped penises. It doesn't matter which direction I move my head because everywhere I look I see penises.” </i> </b></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1215690180" />
    <a title="Sleepless Readmore" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/29809756-sleepless-readmore"><img alt="Sleepless Readmore" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1429608469p2/29809756.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1215690180?book_show_action=true">Mar 01, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sleepless Readmore" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sleepless Readmore" href="/user/show/29809756-sleepless-readmore">Sleepless Readmore</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Sleepless by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/32301543-rin-w-vitale">Rin W. Vitale</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29809756-sleepless-readmore?shelf=5-star-books">5-star-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29809756-sleepless-readmore?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29809756-sleepless-readmore?shelf=all-stars">all-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1215690180" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4907535849029828508">She <i>asked</i> me to tell her <b>the three words</b> <br/>every <u>girl</u> wants to <i>hear</i>. <br/>So I <i>whispered</i>,<br/>"<b>I play hockey</b>" in her ear.<br/><br/><b>5</b> MOTHER PUCKING <b>STARS</b> .. <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424381814ra/13754357.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>Garrett</i> <b>and</b> <i>Hannah</i> ♥<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425775333i/13932754._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>10 Reasons To Date A Hockey Player</b><br/><br/><blockquote>1. They have <b>great</b> hands.<br/>2. They <b>always</b> wear protection.<br/>3. They know when to play <b>rough</b>.<br/>4. They can <b>score</b> from any position.<br/>5. <b>Never</b> stop until the job is done.<br/>6. They love to <b>slam</b> bodies.<br/>7. When the play rough they hit from <b>behind</b>.<br/>8. Tremendous <b>stamina</b> and endurance.<br/>9. Good <b>players</b> score more than once a nigh</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText4907535849029828508" style="display:none">She <i>asked</i> me to tell her <b>the three words</b> <br>every <u>girl</u> wants to <i>hear</i>. <br>So I <i>whispered</i>,<br>"<b>I play hockey</b>" in her ear.<br><br><b>5</b> MOTHER PUCKING <b>STARS</b> .. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424381814ra/13754357.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Garrett</i> <b>and</b> <i>Hannah</i> ♥<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425775333i/13932754._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>10 Reasons To Date A Hockey Player</b><br><br><blockquote>1. They have <b>great</b> hands.<br>2. They <b>always</b> wear protection.<br>3. They know when to play <b>rough</b>.<br>4. They can <b>score</b> from any position.<br>5. <b>Never</b> stop until the job is done.<br>6. They love to <b>slam</b> bodies.<br>7. When the play rough they hit from <b>behind</b>.<br>8. Tremendous <b>stamina</b> and endurance.<br>9. Good <b>players</b> score more than once a night.<br>10. All other athletes like to play with <b>balls</b>.</blockquote><br>And this is why I <u>need</u> a <i>HOCKEY PLAYER</i> .. mind if I <b>borrow yours</b> <i>Hannah</i>?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425775530ra/13932816.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
<i>I</i> was <b>starting</b> to <u>worry</u><br><i>I</i> might <b>actually</b> be <i>your</i> type,<br>and that's too <u>terrifying</u> <br>to even <b>contemplate</b> .."</blockquote><br><br> So .. I don't know <b>WHY</b> but I've had this book for a while in my <i>TBR</i> why it took me till <u>random 4 AM</u> bored-ness to read? Not <i>entirely</i> sure .. somethings <s>WRONG</s> with me. I say this <b>because</b> I have honestly missed out .. THIS NOVEL was F*CKING AMAZING. I haven't read a <i>NA</i> quite as perfection in <i>a long time</i>. <b>FINALLY</b>, I could really connect with these <i>characters</i> and their problems because we're in the <b>same</b> point of our lives. These characters honestly .. were <b>absolutf*ckamazing</b> .. <i>YES, I made that up</i> .. No words in the <s>dictionary</s> would suffice to the <i>level of perfection</i>. The plot was <b>BRILLIANT</b> .. it was believable, <b>emotional</b>, and wonderful. I laughed incredibly loud for someone up at <b>4 AM</b> and then I cried .. not just from the <i>sad parts</i> but from the parts where it was <u>too f*cking cute</u> and your <s>heart can't</s> contain anymore and then <b>BAM</b> cue the <i>waterworks</i>.<br><br><blockquote>When <i>I</i> snicker, <br><i>Garrett</i> pounces like a <b>mountain lion</b>.<br>"<b>Holy shit</b>. Was that a laugh? <br>I didn't think you <s>were capable</s> of <br>showing amusement. <u>Can you</u> do it again<br>and let me <b>film</b> it?"</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425776227ra/13932935.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <blockquote>I don't think you're right for him.<br>Look at what it might have been ..<a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=lL9nytKWg8U" rel="nofollow noopener">►♫</a>
</blockquote>
</i> <br><br><i>Hannah</i> and <i>Garrett</i>'s chemistry was undeniable. The best part is that they <b>built</b> an unbreakable friendship .. they were comfortable around one another. That's what made <i>HER</i> different from all the other girls that <i>Garrett</i>'s been with .. that's what made <u>HER</u> special. He actually <u>wanted</u> her around for a change .. as did his <b>friends</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ESPECIALLY <i>LOGAN</i> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>! They both <b>supported</b> each other and whatever happened whether it was <u>good</u> or <s>bad</s> they came to each <u>other</u>. <s>Football</s> players .. PSSSH who needs one of those .. <i>Hannah</i>, sweetheart .. you lucked out with this <b>one</b> #HockeyOverEverything. <br><br><blockquote>"It <s>breaks</s> my fucking <b>heart</b> to hear you <i>cry</i>."<br>"I'm <u>broken</u>."<br>"You're not <s>broken</s>, <i>baby</i>. I <b>promise</b>."</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425776300ra/13932941.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>".. I <u>know</u> that when she says <b>she loves me</b>,<br>she actually <u>means me</u>-<i>Garrett</i>-and not<br>Briar's <i>hockey</i> star, or Mr. <b>Popularity</b>,<br>or <s>Phil Graham</s>'s son. <br><i>She loves me</i>.</blockquote><br><br>Most <i>NA</i> books include some heavy a*s topics .. with that being said, this was one of those. <b>HOWEVER</b>, I loved how <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1935000.Elle_Kennedy" title="Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">Elle Kennedy</a> went with it. These characters were <i>broken</i> and still <i>mending</i> but the process was sped up when they had <b>EACH OTHER</b>. The scenarios were <i>believable</i> and not over the <b>top</b>. <br><br><i>
  <blockquote>I belong with you, <br>You belong with me, <br>You're my sweetheart ..<a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=lL9nytKWg8U" rel="nofollow noopener">►♫</a>
</blockquote>
</i><br><br>This wasn't my first from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1935000.Elle_Kennedy" title="Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">Elle Kennedy</a> and not going to be my <b>LAST</b>. The first was <b>another</b> hockey book by her <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5830579.Body_Check" title="Body Check by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">Body Check</a> .. she knows her <b>sh*t</b> about these hockey <i>players</i>. When I <b>came across</b> this book .. I knew the name looked familiar and I can <u>honestly say</u> that this <i>author</i> has <b>progressed</b> and will hopefully <i>continue</i> to share this <b>unbelievable</b> talent. I <b>CANNOT</b> WAIT FOR THE <b>NEXT</b> ONE #GiveItToMePlease. This book was <b>recommended</b> to me .. and shout out to <i>RIN</i>, <u>THANK YOU</u>. If your hesitant to read .. <b>JUST READ IT</b> .. <i>I KNOW YOU WANT TOO</i>. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425776227ra/13932936.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24504048.The_Deal__Off_Campus___1_" title="The Deal (Off-Campus, #1) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">The Deal</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1935000.Elle_Kennedy" title="Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">Elle Kennedy</a><br><i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/29809756-sleepless-readmore" rel="nofollow noopener">- Sleepless, Readmore.</a>
</i> <i>
  <a href="https://twitter.com/sleepread_" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a>
</i><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24504048.The_Deal__Off_Campus___1_" title="The Deal (Off-Campus, #1) by Elle Kennedy" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1423753287s/24504048.jpg" alt="The Deal (Off-Campus, #1) by Elle Kennedy" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1268095646" />
    <a title="Angela" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30035966-angela"><img alt="Angela" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1523817330p2/30035966.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1268095646?book_show_action=true">Apr 30, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela" href="/user/show/30035966-angela">Angela</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30035966-angela?shelf=5-star-favorites">5-star-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1268095646" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11999392341037430705"><b>You ask "What has all the countless amount of hours reading taught you?"<br/>I reply "That usually the worst the book cover is better the book will be."</b><br/><br/>Okay, so that might not always be the case but it was for <i> The Deal</i>.<br/><br/>I kept seeing people say that this "is new adult done right"... and they are right this is new adult done right. Since we're all friends here I feel okay openly saying this... 99% of the time when it comes to new adult you know what you're getting yourself into. And 99% of the time th</span>
  <span id="freeText11999392341037430705" style="display:none"><b>You ask "What has all the countless amount of hours reading taught you?"<br>I reply "That usually the worst the book cover is better the book will be."</b><br><br>Okay, so that might not always be the case but it was for <i> The Deal</i>.<br><br>I kept seeing people say that this "is new adult done right"... and they are right this is new adult done right. Since we're all friends here I feel okay openly saying this... 99% of the time when it comes to new adult you know what you're getting yourself into. And 99% of the time that's why you pick it up! You want a light, fluffy, fun book that will steal your heart and take you away from reality for a few hours. This book did that for me. I had so much fun reading it. There wasn't a story-line or plot twist I didn't see coming, and the story still had me giddy and blushing.<br><br><b>
  <i>"I never expected her. Sometimes people sneak up on you and suddenly you don't know how you ever lived without them. How you went about your day and hung out with your friends and fucked other people without having this one important person in your life."</i>
</b><br><br><br>(Secretly) Sometimes I like when I push reading a book off because I judged it by it's cover, because I like when I finally cave in, read it, and it ends up being a pleasant surprise... Hell I even like when I say "Dang, mad I put that off for so long."<br><br><i> The Deal </i> had me thinking exactly that. I loved how real this book felt. I loved how raw the characters are. I loved how full of life their relationship is. And I loved the banter and jokes these two throw at each other. My two favorite things however are: First, that Elle could have taken this down the path of insta-love but decided to build a relationship that started legit as a friendship and built up to more. Two, the moment she had the lead say "Kiss the crap out of her" and I got to bust up laughing because it automatically made me think of that scene in She's the Man...<br><br><div>
  <br>
  <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-zfCK9EYB7Uc/VkkzJk45OPI/AAAAAAAACiw/pU6U6oaDIQk/s1600/shes%2Bthe%2Bman.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447638091ra/17031401.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div><br><br>If you're looking for a good romancey roll around in the sheet read, this is the read for you.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11999392341037430705" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('7PGurm8yVNHJ69enFSwl/MpUaHR67Ie50yt6IHH79p1XbrXQYJJlBjBL5hR4Gb2GUEiOCK0s3eaBnX0EO6Wi+Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('gyV0u4a5nHnKZDzHYZmA4kbeQ8qUw9ng14RHdvEG3FY4um/FiRmtrjPEDXQMrBiY3MKltkMDg7+FMkBSu1iIMg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
